  764   
  765   static const mxArray *c_emlrt_marshallOut(real_T u_data[25], int32_T u_size[1])
  766   {
  767     const mxArray *y;
  768     static const int32_T iv75[1] = { 0 };
  769   
  770     const mxArray *m18;
  771     y = NULL;
  772     m18 = mxCreateNumericArray(1, (int32_T *)&iv75, mxDOUBLE_CLASS, mxREAL);
  773     mxSetData((mxArray *)m18, (void *)u_data);
  774     mxSetDimensions((mxArray *)m18, u_size, 1);
  775     emlrtAssign(&y, m18);
  776     return y;
  777   }

  780   {

 1417   static const mxArray *d_emlrt_marshallOut(real_T u_data[625], int32_T u_size[2])
 1418   {
 1419     const mxArray *y;
 1420     static const int32_T iv76[2] = { 0, 0 };
 1421   
 1422     const mxArray *m19;
 1423     y = NULL;
 1424     m19 = mxCreateNumericArray(2, (int32_T *)&iv76, mxDOUBLE_CLASS, mxREAL);
 1425     mxSetData((mxArray *)m19, (void *)u_data);
 1426     mxSetDimensions((mxArray *)m19, u_size, 2);
 1427     emlrtAssign(&y, m19);
 1428     return y;
 1429   }

 2043   static void e_emlrt_marshallIn(const mxArray *xk, const char_T *identifier,
 2044     real_T (**y_data)[25], int32_T y_size[1])
 2045   {
 2046     emlrtMsgIdentifier thisId;
 2047     thisId.fIdentifier = identifier;
 2048     thisId.fParent = NULL;
 2049     f_emlrt_marshallIn(emlrtAlias(xk), &thisId, y_data, y_size);
 2050     emlrtDestroyArray(&xk);
 2051   }

 3282   static void g_emlrt_marshallIn(const mxArray *Pxk, const char_T *identifier,
 3283     real_T (**y_data)[625], int32_T y_size[2])
 3284   {
 3285     emlrtMsgIdentifier thisId;
 3286     thisId.fIdentifier = identifier;
 3287     thisId.fParent = NULL;
 3288     h_emlrt_marshallIn(emlrtAlias(Pxk), &thisId, y_data, y_size);
 3289     emlrtDestroyArray(&Pxk);
 3290   }

 3908   static void h_emlrt_marshallIn(const mxArray *u, const emlrtMsgIdentifier
 3909     *parentId, real_T (**y_data)[625], int32_T y_size[2])
 3910   {
 3911     p_emlrt_marshallIn(emlrtAlias(u), parentId, y_data, y_size);
 3912     emlrtDestroyArray(&u);
 3913   }

 3915   static void h_info_helper(ResolvedFunctionInfo info[562])

 4545   static void i_emlrt_marshallIn(const mxArray *Pnk, const char_T *identifier,
 4546     emxArray_real_T *y)
 4547   {
 4548     emlrtMsgIdentifier thisId;
 4549     thisId.fIdentifier = identifier;
 4550     thisId.fParent = NULL;
 4551     j_emlrt_marshallIn(emlrtAlias(Pnk), &thisId, y);
 4552     emlrtDestroyArray(&Pnk);
 4553   }

 5759   void ukf_update_17_state_api(const mxArray * const prhs[7], const mxArray *plhs
 5760     [2])
 5761   {
 5762     real_T (*xnew_data)[25];
 5763     real_T (*Pnew_data)[625];
 5764     emxArray_real_T *Pnk;
 5765     int32_T xk_size[1];
 5766     real_T (*xk_data)[25];
 5767     int32_T Pxk_size[2];
 5768     real_T (*Pxk_data)[625];
 5769     int32_T Pvk_size[2];
 5770     real_T (*Pvk_data)[625];
 5771     int32_T uk_size[1];
 5772     real_T (*uk_data)[250];
 5773     int32_T ytilde_size[1];
 5774     real_T (*ytilde_data)[250];
 5775     real_T alpha;
 5776     const mxArray *tmp;
 5777     int32_T Pnew_size[2];
 5778     int32_T xnew_size[1];
 5779     xnew_data = (real_T (*)[25])mxMalloc(sizeof(real_T [25]));
 5780     Pnew_data = (real_T (*)[625])mxMalloc(sizeof(real_T [625]));
 5781     emlrtHeapReferenceStackEnterFcnR2012b(emlrtRootTLSGlobal);
 5782     emxInit_real_T(&Pnk, 2, &sb_emlrtRTEI, TRUE);
 5783   
 5784     /* Marshall function inputs */
 5785     e_emlrt_marshallIn(emlrtAlias(prhs[0]), "xk", &xk_data, xk_size);
 5786     g_emlrt_marshallIn(emlrtAlias(prhs[1]), "Pxk", &Pxk_data, Pxk_size);
 5787     g_emlrt_marshallIn(emlrtAlias(prhs[2]), "Pvk", &Pvk_data, Pvk_size);
 5788     i_emlrt_marshallIn(emlrtAlias(prhs[3]), "Pnk", Pnk);
 5789     k_emlrt_marshallIn(emlrtAlias(prhs[4]), "uk", &uk_data, uk_size);
 5790     k_emlrt_marshallIn(emlrtAlias(prhs[5]), "ytilde", &ytilde_data, ytilde_size);
 5791     alpha = emlrt_marshallIn(emlrtAliasP(prhs[6]), "alpha");
 5792   
 5793     /* Marshall in global variables */
 5794     tmp = mexGetVariable("global", "Ts");
 5795     if (tmp) {
 5796       Ts = emlrt_marshallIn(tmp, "Ts");
 5797       Ts_dirty = 0U;
 5798     }
 5799   
 5800     /* Invoke the target function */
 5801     ukf_update_17_state(*xk_data, xk_size, *Pxk_data, Pxk_size, *Pvk_data,
 5802                         Pvk_size, Pnk, *uk_data, uk_size, *ytilde_data,
 5803                         ytilde_size, alpha, *xnew_data, xnew_size, *Pnew_data,
 5804                         Pnew_size);
 5805   
 5806     /* Marshall out global variables */
 5807     mexPutVariable("global", "Ts", emlrt_marshallOut(Ts));
 5808   
 5809     /* Marshall function outputs */
 5810     plhs[0] = c_emlrt_marshallOut(*xnew_data, xnew_size);
 5811     plhs[1] = d_emlrt_marshallOut(*Pnew_data, Pnew_size);
 5812     Pnk->canFreeData = FALSE;
 5813     emxFree_real_T(&Pnk);
 5814     emlrtHeapReferenceStackLeaveFcnR2012b(emlrtRootTLSGlobal);
 5815   }
